[cystic_vein.n.01] cystic vein -- vein that drains the gallbladder
[cystine.n.01] cystine -- a crystalline amino acid found in proteins (especially keratin); discovered in bladder stones
[cystitis.n.01] cystitis -- inflammation of the urinary bladder and ureters
[cyst.n.01] cyst -- a closed sac that develops abnormally in some body structure
[cystocele.n.01] cystocele -- hernia in which the urinary bladder protrudes through the wall of the vagina; sometimes occurs after childbirth
[cystoid_macular_edema.n.01] cystoid macular edema -- a specific pattern of swelling in the central retina Also a hyponym of: eye_disease.n.01.
[cystophora.n.01] Cystophora -- hooded seals
[cystoplegia.n.01] cystoplegia -- paralysis of the urinary bladder
[cystopteris.n.01] Cystopteris -- chiefly small perennial rock ferns: bladder ferns; in some classifications placed in Polypodiaceae
[cytisus.n.01] Cytisus -- large genus of stiff or spiny evergreen or deciduous Old World shrubs: broom
[cytoarchitecture.n.01] cytoarchitecture -- the cellular composition of a bodily structure
[cytochrome_c.n.01] cytochrome c -- the most abundant and stable cytochrome; involved in energy transfer
[cytochrome.n.01] cytochrome -- (biochemistry) a class of hemoprotein whose principal biological function is electron transfer (especially in cellular respiration)
[cytogenesis.n.01] cytogenesis -- the origin and development and variation of cells
[cytogeneticist.n.01] cytogeneticist -- a geneticist who specializes in the cellular components associated with heredity
[cytogenetics.n.01] cytogenetics -- the branch of biology that studies the cellular aspects of heredity (especially the chromosomes) Also a hyponym of: genetics.n.01.
[cytokine.n.01] cytokine -- any of various protein molecules secreted by cells of the immune system that serve to regulate the immune system
[cytokinesis.n.01] cytokinesis -- organic process consisting of the division of the cytoplasm of a cell following karyokinesis bringing about the separation into two daughter cells
[cytologic_specimen.n.01] cytologic specimen -- a specimen used for cytologic examination and diagnosis
[cytologist.n.01] cytologist -- a biologist who studies the structure and function of cells
[cytology.n.01] cytology -- the branch of biology that studies the structure and function of cells Also a hyponym of: microscopic_anatomy.n.01.
[cytolysin.n.01] cytolysin -- a substance that partly or completely destroys animal cells
[cytolysis.n.01] cytolysis -- pathological breakdown of cells by the destruction of their outer membrane
[cytomegalovirus.n.01] cytomegalovirus -- any of a group of herpes viruses that enlarge epithelial cells and can cause birth defects; can affect humans with impaired immunological systems
[cytopenia.n.01] cytopenia -- a deficiency of some cellular element of the blood
[cytophotometer.n.01] cytophotometer -- a photometer that can be used to locate and identify chemical compounds in a cell by measuring the intensity of the light that passes through stained sections of the cytoplasm
[cytophotometry.n.01] cytophotometry -- the study of chemical compounds inside a cell by means of a cytophotometer
[cytoplasm.n.01] cytoplasm -- the protoplasm of a cell excluding the nucleus; is full of proteins that control cell metabolism
[cytoplast.n.01] cytoplast -- the intact cytoplasmic content of a cell
[cytosine.n.01] cytosine -- a base found in DNA and RNA and derived from pyrimidine; pairs with guanine
[cytoskeleton.n.01] cytoskeleton -- a microscopic network of actin filaments and microtubules in the cytoplasm of many living cells that gives the cell shape and coherence
[cytosol.n.01] cytosol -- the aqueous part of the cytoplasm within which various particles and organelles are suspended
[cytostome.n.01] cytostome -- mouth of a protozoan
[cytotoxic_drug.n.01] cytotoxic drug -- any drug that has a toxic effect on cells; commonly used in chemotherapy to inhibit the proliferation of cancerous cells
[cytotoxicity.n.01] cytotoxicity -- the degree to which something is toxic to living cells
[cytotoxin.n.01] cytotoxin -- any substance that has a toxic effect on cells

[czar.n.01] czar -- a male monarch or emperor (especially of Russia prior to 1917)
[czar.n.02] czar -- a person having great power
[czech_monetary_unit.n.01] Czech monetary unit -- monetary unit in Czech Republic
[czech.n.01] Czech -- a native of inhabitant of the Czech Republic

[czerny.n.01] Czerny -- Austrian virtuoso pianist and composer of many works for the piano; studied with Beethoven and was a teacher of Liszt (1791-1857) Also a hyponym of: pianist.n.01.
[czestochowa.n.01] Czestochowa -- a city of southern Poland whose church contains the statue of the black Madonna which attracts many pilgrims
